He left the United Kingdom for the United States in the late 1970s, citing the <a href="/wiki/Income_tax" title="Income tax">income tax</a> levied on top earners by the <a href="/wiki/Labour_Party_(UK)" title="Labour Party (UK)">Labour</a> government of <a href="/wiki/James_Callaghan" title="James Callaghan">James Callaghan</a>, which then stood at 83%,<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> but returned to the UK eight years later when taxes had been lowered by the <a href="/wiki/Conservative_Party_(UK)" title="Conservative Party (UK)">Conservative</a> government of <a href="/wiki/Margaret_Thatcher" title="Margaret Thatcher">Margaret Thatcher</a>:\n</p>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r856303468"/><blockquote class="templatequote"><p>I realised that\'s not a socialist country, it\'s a communist country without a dictator, so I left and I was never going to come back. Maggie Thatcher came in and put the taxes back down and in the end, you know, you don\'t mind paying tax. What am I going to do? Not pay tax and drive around in a <a href="/wiki/Rolls-Royce_(car)" class="mw-redirect" title="Rolls-Royce (car)">Rolls-Royce</a>, with cripples begging on the street like you see in some countries?<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup>\n</p></blockquote>\n<p>Following the launch of his film <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Brown_(film)" title="Harry Brown (film)">Harry Brown</a></i>, Caine called for the reintroduction of <a href="/wiki/National_service" title="National service">national service</a> in the UK to give young people "a sense of belonging, rather than a sense of violence".<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>In 2009, Caine publicly criticised the Labour government of <a href="/wiki/Gordon_Brown" title="Gordon Brown">Gordon Brown</a> for its new 50% income tax rate on top earners and threatened to return to the US if his taxes were increased further.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup> During the run up to the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_general_election,_2010" title="United Kingdom general election, 2010">2010 General Election</a>, Caine publicly endorsed the <a href="/wiki/Conservative_Party_(UK)" title="Conservative Party (UK)">Conservative Party</a> and appeared with party leader <a href="/wiki/David_Cameron" title="David Cameron">David Cameron</a> for the launch of a civilian non-compulsory "National Service" for 16-year-olds, although Caine stated he had previously supported <a href="/wiki/New_Labour" title="New Labour">New Labour</a> under the leadership of <a href="/wiki/Tony_Blair" title="Tony Blair">Tony Blair</a> in <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_general_election,_1997" title="United Kingdom general election, 1997">1997</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup> In July 2014, Caine was reported to have been a celebrity investor in a tax avoidance scheme called Liberty.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> Caine also voted for <a href="/wiki/Brexit" title="Brexit">Brexit</a>, stating he would rather be a "poor master than a rich servant".<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Music_interests">Music interests</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Michael_Caine&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Music interests">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>Caine is a fan of <a href="/wiki/Chill-out_music" title="Chill-out music">chill-out music</a>, and released a compilation CD called <i>Cained</i> in 2007 on the <a href="/wiki/UMTV" class="mw-redirect" title="UMTV">UMTV</a> record label.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-wiredcained_84-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-wiredcained-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup> He met <a href="/wiki/Elton_John" title="Elton John">Elton John</a> and was discussing musical tastes, when Caine said that he had been creating chillout <a href="/wiki/Mixtape" title="Mixtape">mix tapes</a> as an amateur for years.<sup id="cite_ref-wiredcained_84-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-wiredcained-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup> Also in music, Caine provided vocal samples for the Ska-pop band <a href="/wiki/Madness_(band)" title="Madness (band)">Madness</a> for their 1984 hit "<a href="/wiki/Michael_Caine_(song)" title="Michael Caine (song)">Michael Caine</a>", as his daughter was a fan. He has sung in film roles as well, including <i><a href="/wiki/Little_Voice_(film)" title="Little Voice (film)">Little Voice</a></i> and for the 1992 musical film <i><a href="/wiki/The_Muppet_Christmas_Carol" title="The Muppet Christmas Carol">The Muppet Christmas Carol</a></i>.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Filmography">Filmography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Michael_Caine&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Filmography">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Michael_Caine_filmography" title="Michael Caine filmography">Michael Caine filmography</a></div>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Awards_and_honours">Awards and honours</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Michael_Caine&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Awards and honours">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Michael_Caine_handprints,_Leicester_Square_WC2_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1352187.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/Michael_Caine_handprints%2C_Leicester_Square_WC2_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1352187.jpg/200px-Michael_Caine_handprints%2C_Leicester_Square_WC2_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1352187.jpg" width="200" height="150" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/Michael_Caine_handprints%2C_Leicester_Square_WC2_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1352187.jpg/300px-Michael_Caine_handprints%2C_Leicester_Square_WC2_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1352187.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/Michael_Caine_handprints%2C_Leicester_Square_WC2_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1352187.jpg/400px-Michael_Caine_handprints%2C_Leicester_Square_WC2_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1352187.jpg 2x" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="480" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Michael_Caine_handprints,_Leicester_Square_WC2_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1352187.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Michael Caine\'s handprints in <a href="/wiki/Leicester_Square" title="Leicester Square">Leicester Square</a>, London</div></div></div>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Michael_Caine" title="List of awards and nominations received by Michael Caine">List of awards and nominations received by Michael Caine</a></div>\n<p>Caine has been nominated for an Oscar six times, winning his first <a href="/wiki/Academy_Awards" title="Academy Awards">Academy Award</a> for the 1986 film <i>Hannah and Her Sisters</i>, and his second in 1999 for <i>The Cider House Rules</i>, in both cases as a supporting actor. His performance in <i>Educating Rita</i> in 1983 earned him the <a href="/wiki/BAFTA_Award_for_Best_Actor_in_a_Leading_Role" title="BAFTA Award for Best Actor in a Leading Role">BAFTA</a> and <a href="/wiki/Golden_Globe_Award_for_Best_Actor_%E2%80%93_Motion_Picture_Musical_or_Comedy" title="Golden Globe Award for Best Actor \xe2\x80\x93 Motion Picture Musical or Comedy">Golden Globe Award for Best Actor</a>. Caine is one of only two actors nominated for an Academy Award for acting in every decade from the 1960s to 2000s (the other one being <a href="/wiki/Jack_Nicholson" title="Jack Nicholson">Jack Nicholson</a>); <a href="/wiki/Laurence_Olivier" title="Laurence Olivier">Laurence Olivier</a> was also nominated for an acting Academy Award in five different decades, beginning in 1939 and ending in 1978, as has <a href="/wiki/Paul_Newman" title="Paul Newman">Paul Newman</a> (1950s, \'60s, \'80s, \'90s and 2000s). Caine appeared in seven films that were ranked in the <a href="/wiki/British_Film_Institute" title="British Film Institute">BFI</a>\'s <a href="/wiki/BFI_Top_100_British_films" title="BFI Top 100 British films">100 greatest British films of the 20th century</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>He was appointed <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_British_Empire" title="Order of the British Empire">Commander of the Order of the British Empire</a> (CBE) in the 1992 <a href="/wiki/Birthday_Honours" title="Birthday Honours">Queen\'s Birthday Honours</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> and in the <a href="/wiki/2000_Birthday_Honours" title="2000 Birthday Honours">2000 Birthday Honours</a> he was <a href="/wiki/Knight_Bachelor" title="Knight Bachelor">knighted</a> as <i>Sir Maurice Micklewhite CBE</i> by Queen <a href="/wiki/Elizabeth_II" title="Elizabeth II">Elizabeth II</a> at Buckingham Palace.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> In a tribute to his background, he stated: "I was named after my father and I was knighted in his name because I love my father. I always kept my real name\xe2\x80\x94I\'m a very private and family-orientated person."<sup id="cite_ref-knighted_90-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-knighted-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup> In 2000 he received a <a href="/wiki/BAFTA_Fellowship" title="BAFTA Fellowship">BAFTA Academy Fellowship Award</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>In 2008, Caine was awarded the prize for Outstanding Contribution to Showbusiness at the <a href="/wiki/Variety_Club" class="mw-redirect" title="Variety Club">Variety Club</a> Awards.<sup id="cite_ref-Variety_92-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Variety-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup> On 5 January 2011 he was made a Commander of the <a href="/wiki/Ordre_des_Arts_et_des_Lettres" title="Ordre des Arts et des Lettres">Ordre des Arts et des Lettres</a> by France\'s culture minister, <a href="/wiki/Fr%C3%A9d%C3%A9ric_Mitterrand" title="Fr\xc3\xa9d\xc3\xa9ric Mitterrand">Fr\xc3\xa9d\xc3\xa9ric Mitterrand</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup> In May 2012, Caine was awarded the Honorary <a href="/wiki/Freedom_of_the_City" title="Freedom of the City">Freedom</a> of the <a href="/wiki/London_Borough_of_Southwark" title="London Borough of Southwark">London Borough of Southwark</a> as a person of distinction and eminence of the borough.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="References">References</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Michael_Caine&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit
